          version INTEGER NOT NULL\n137\t            )\",\n138\t            &[] as &[&dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n139\t        )?;\n140\t\n141\t        // Check current version\n142\t        let current_version: Option<i64> = conn\n143\t            .query_row(\n144\t                \"SELECT version FROM schema_version\",\n145\t                &[] as &[&dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n146\t                |row| row.get(0),\n147\t            )\n148\t            .ok();\n149\t\n150\t        if current_version.is_none() {\n151\t            // Initialize schema\n152\t            Self::init_schema(&conn)?;\n153\t            conn.execute(\n154\t                \"INSERT INTO schema_version (version) VALUES (1)\",\n155\t                &[] as &[&dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n156\t            )?;\n157\t        } else if current_version != Some(SCHEMA_VERSION) {\n158\t            return Err(TaskStoreError::InvalidData(format!(\n159\t                \"schema version mismatch: expected {}, got {}\",\n160\t                SCHEMA_VERSION,\n161\t                current_version.unwrap()\n162\t            )));\n163\t        }\n164\t\n165\t        Ok(())\n166\t    }\n167\t\n168\t    async |row| row.get(0),\n173\t        )\n174\t    }\n175\t\n176\t    async fn task_insert(&self, task: &Task) -> Result<()> {\n177\t        let node_tasks_json = }\n545\t\n546\t    async fn job_dequeue(&self, worker_id: &str) -> Result<Option<Job>> {\n547\t        // Start a transaction\n548\t        let conn = self\n549\t            .conn\n550\t            .lock()\n551\t            .map_err(|e| TaskStoreError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n552\t        let tx = conn.unchecked_transaction()?;\n553\t\n554\t        let now = chrono::Utc::now().timestamp_millis() as u64;\n555\t        let expires_at = now + (5 * 60 * 1000); // 5 minutes from now\n556\t\n557\t        // Find and claim a job\n558\t        let job_id: Option<String> = tx\n559\t            .query_row(\n560\t                \"SELECT id FROM jobs WHERE state = 'queued' ORDER BY id ASC LIMIT 1\",\n561\t                [],\n562\t                |row| row.get(0),\n563\t            )\n564\t            .ok();\n565\t\n566\t        if let Some(ref job_id) = job_id {\n567\t            tx.execute(\n568\t                \"UPDATE jobs SET state = 'in_progress', claimed_by = ?1, claim_expires_at = ?2 WHERE id = ?3\",\n569\t                [\n570\t                    &worker_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n571\t                    &expires_at as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n572\t                    job_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n573\t                ],\n574\t            )?;\n575\t\n576\t            // Fetch the updated job\n577\t            let job: Job = tx.query_row(\n578\t                \"SELECT id, type, params, state, claimed_by, claim_expires_at, progress\n579\t                 FROM jobs WHERE id = ?1\",\n580\t                [job_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n581\t                |row| {\n582\t                    Ok(Job {\n583\t                        id: row.get(0)?,\n584\t                        job_type: row.get(1)?,\n585\t                        params: row.get(2)?,\n586\t                        state: row.get::<_, String>(3)?.parse().map_err(parse_error)?,\n587\t                        claimed_by: {\n588\t                            let claimed: String = row.get(4)?;\n589\t                            if claimed.is_empty() {\n590\t                                None\n591\t                            } else {\n592\t                                Some(claimed)\n593\t                            }\n594\t                        },\n595\t                        claim_expires_at: {\n596\t                            let expires: i64 = row.get(5)?;\n597\t                            if expires == 0 {\n598\t                                None\n599\t                            } else {\n600\t                                Some(expires as u64)\n601\t                            }\n602\t                        },\n603\t                        progress: row.get(6)?,\n604\t                    })\n605\t                },\n606\t            )?;\n607\t\n608\t            tx.commit()?;\n609\t            Ok(Some(job))\n610\t        } else {\n611\t            tx.commit()?;\n612\t            Ok(None)\n613\t        }\n614\t    }\n615\t\n616\t    async fn job_update_status(\n617\t        &self,\n618\t        job_id: &str,\n619\t        status: JobState,\n620\t        result: Option<&str>,\n621\t    ) -> Result<()> {\n622\t        self.execute(\n623\t            \"UPDATE jobs SET state = ?1, progress = ?2 WHERE id = ?3\",\n624\t            &[\n625\t                &status.to_string(),\n626\t  }\n668\t\n669\t    async fn job_list(&self, status: Option<JobState>, limit: usize) -> Result<Vec<Job>> {\n670\t        let mut sql =\n671\t            \"SELECT id, type, params, state, claimed_by, claim_expires_at, progress FROM jobs\"\n672\t                .to_string();\n673\t\n674\t        if status.is_some() {\n675\t            sql.push_str(\" WHERE state = ?\");\n676\t        }\n677\t\n678\t        sql.push_str(&format!(\" ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT {limit}\"));\n679\t\n680\t        let status_str: Option<String> = status.map(|s| s.to_string());\n681\t        let params: Vec<&dyn rusqlite::ToSql> = match &status_str {\n682\t            Some(s) => vec![s],\n683\t            None => vec![],\n684\t        };\n685\t\n686\t        self.query_map(&sql, &params, |row| {\n687\t            Ok(Job {\n688\t                id: row.get(0)?,\n689\t                job_type: row.get(1)?,\n690\t                params: row.get(2)?,\n691\t                state: row.get::<_, String>(3)?.parse().map_err(parse_error)?,\n692\t                claimed_by: {\n693\t                    let claimed: String = row.get(4)?;\n694\t                    if claimed.is_empty() {\n695\t                        None\n696\t                    } else {\n697\t                        Some(claimed)\n698\t                    }\n699\t                },\n700\t                claim_expires_at: {\n701\t                    let expires: i64 = row.get(5)?;\n702\t                    if expires == 0 {\n703\t                        None\n704\t                    } else {\n705\t                        Some(expires as u64)\n706\t                    }\n707\t                },\n708\t                progress: row.get(6)?,\n709\t            })\n710\t        })\n711\t    }\n712\t\n713\t    async fn leader_lease_acquire(&self, lease: &LeaderLease) -> Result<bool> {\n714\t        let conn = self\n715\t            .conn\n716\t            .lock()\n717\t            .map_err(|e| TaskStoreError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n718\t        let tx = conn.unchecked_transaction()?;\n719\t\n720\t        let now = chrono::Utc::now().timestamp_millis() as u64;\n721\t\n722\t        // Check if there's an existing valid lease for this scope\n723\t        let existing: Option<(String, u64)> = tx\n724\t            .query_row(\n725\t                \"SELECT scope, expires_at FROM leader_lease WHERE scope = ?1 AND expires_at > ?2\",\n726\t                [&lease.scope as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql, &now as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n727\t                |row| Ok((row.get(0)?, row.get(1)?)),\n728\t            )\n729\t            .ok();\n730\t\n731\t        let acquired = if existing.is_some() {\n732\t            false\n733\t        } else {\n734\t            tx.execute(\n735\t                \"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO leader_lease (scope, holder, expires_at)\n736\t                 VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3)\",\n737\t                [\n738\t                    &lease.scope as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n739\t                    &lease.holder,\n740\t                    &lease.expires_at,\n741\t                ],\n742\t            )?;\n743\t            true\n744\t        };\n745\t\n746\t        tx.commit()?;\n747\t        Ok(acquired)\n748\t    }\n749\t\n750\t    async fn leader_lease_release(&self, scope: &str) -> Result<()> {\n751\t         |row| {\n                let target_uids_json: String = row.get(3)?;\n                // Handle null case for single-target aliases\n                let target_uids: Option<Vec<String>> = if serde_json::from_str(&target_uids_json).map_err(|e| rusqlite::Error::ToSqlConversionFailure(Box::new(e)))?;\n                    Some(parsed)\n                };\n                let history_json: String = row.get(6)?;\n                let history: Vec<super::schema::AliasHistoryEntry> =\n                    serde_json::from_str(&history_json)\n                        .map_err(|e| rusqlite::Error::ToSqlConversionFailure(Box::new(e)))?;\n                Ok(Alias {\n                    name: row.get(0)?,\n                    kind: row.get::<_, String>(1)?.parse().map_err(|e| {\n                        parse_error(e)\n                    })?,\n                    current_uid: {\n                        let uid: String = row.get(2)?;\n                        if uid.is_empty() { None } else { Some(uid) }\n                    },\n                    target_uids,\n                    version: row.get(4)?,\n                    created_at: row.get(5)?,\n                    history,\n                })\n            },\n        )\n    }\n\n    async fn session_upsert(&self, session: &Session) -> Result<()> {\n        self.execute(\n            \"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO sessions (session_id, last_write_mtask_id, last_write_at, pinned_group, min_settings_version, ttl)\n             VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, ?4, ?5, ?6)\",\n            &[\n                &session.session_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n                &session.last_write_mtask_id.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"\"),\n                &session.last_write_at.map(|v| v as i64).unwrap_or(0),\n                &session.pinned_group,\n                &session.min_settings_version,\n                &(session.ttl as i64),\n            ] as &[&dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n        )?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n don't have an 'index' field anymore\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn idempotency_check(&self, key: &str) -> Result<Option<IdempotencyEntry>> {\n        let result: Option<IdempotencyEntry> = job_enqueue(&self, job: &Job) -> Result<()> {\n        self.execute(\n            \"INSERT INTO jobs (id, type, params, state, claimed_by, claim_expires_at, progress)\n             VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, ?4, ?5, ?6, ?7)\",\n            &[\n                &job.id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n                &job.job_type,\n                &job.params,\n                &job.state.to_string(),\n                &job.claimed_by.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"\"),\n                &job.claim_expires_at.map(|v| v as i64).unwrap_or(0),\n                &job.progress,\n            ] as &[&dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n        )?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn job_dequeue(&self, worker_id: &str) -> Result<Option<Job>> {\n        // Start a transaction\n        let conn = self\n            .conn\n            .lock()\n            .map_err(|e| TaskStoreError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n        let tx = conn.unchecked_transaction()?;\n\n        let now = chrono::Utc::now().timestamp_millis() as u64;\n        let expires_at = now + (5 * 60 * 1000); // 5 minutes from now\n\n        // Find and claim a job\n        let job_id: Option<String> = tx\n            .query_row(\n                \"SELECT id FROM jobs WHERE state = 'queued' ORDER BY id ASC LIMIT 1\",\n                [],\n                |row| row.get(0),\n            )\n            .ok();\n\n        if let Some(ref job_id) = job_id {\n            tx.execute(\n                \"UPDATE jobs SET state = 'in_progress', claimed_by = ?1, claim_expires_at = ?2 WHERE id = ?3\",\n                [\n                    &worker_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n                    &expires_at as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n                    job_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n                ],\n            )?;\n\n            // Fetch the updated job\n            let job: Job = tx.query_row(\n                \"SELECT id, type, params, state, claimed_by, claim_expires_at, progress\n                 FROM jobs WHERE id = ?1\",\n                [job_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n                |row| {\n                    Ok(Job {\n                        id: row.get(0)?,\n                        job_type: row.get(1)?,\n                        params: row.get(2)?,\n                        state: row.get::<_, String>(3)?.parse().map_err(parse_error)?,\n                        claimed_by: {\n                            let claimed: String = row.get(4)?;\n                            if claimed.is_empty() {\n                                None\n                            } else {\n                                Some(claimed)\n                            }\n                        },\n                        claim_expires_at: {\n                            let expires: i64 = row.get(5)?;\n                            if expires == 0 {\n                                None\n                            } else {\n                                Some(expires as u64)\n                            }\n                        },\n                        progress: row.get(6)?,\n                    })\n                },\n            )?;\n\n            tx.commit()?;\n            Ok(Some(job))\n        } else {\n            tx.commit()?;\n            Ok(None)\n        }\n    }\n\n    async fn job_update_status(\n        &self,\n        job_id: &str,\n        status: JobState,\n        result: Option<&str>,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        self.execute(\n            \"UPDATE jobs SET state = ?1, progress = ?2 WHERE id = ?3\",\n            &[\n                &status.to_string(),\n                &result.unwrap_or(\"\").to_string(),\n                &job_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n            ],\n        )?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn job_get(&self, job_id: &str) -> Result<Option<Job>> {\n        let result: Option<Job> = self\n            .query_row(\n                \"SELECT id, type, params, state, claimed_by, claim_expires_at, progress\n                 FROM jobs WHERE id = ?1\",\n                &[&job_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n                |row| {\n                    Ok(Job {\n                        id: row.get(0)?,\n                        job_type: row.get(1)?,\n                        params: row.get(2)?,\n                        state: row.get::<_, String>(3)?.parse().map_err(parse_error)?,\n                        claimed_by: {\n                            let claimed: String = row.get(4)?;\n                            if claimed.is_empty() {\n                                None\n                            } else {\n                                Some(claimed)\n                            }\n                        },\n                        claim_expires_at: {\n                            let expires: i64 = row.get(5)?;\n                            if expires == 0 {\n                                None\n                            } else {\n                                Some(expires as u64)\n                            }\n                        },\n                        progress: row.get(6)?,\n                    })\n                },\n            )\n            .ok();\n        Ok(result)\n    }\n\n    async fn job_list(&self, status: Option<JobState>, limit: usize) -> Result<Vec<Job>> {\n        let mut sql =\n            \"SELECT id, type, params, state, claimed_by, claim_expires_at, progress FROM jobs\"\n                .to_string();\n\n        if status.is_some() {\n            sql.push_str(\" WHERE state = ?\");\n        }\n\n        sql.push_str(&format!(\" ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT {limit}\"));\n\n        let status_str: Option<String> = status.map(|s| s.to_string());\n        let params: Vec<&dyn rusqlite::ToSql> = match &status_str {\n            Some(s) => vec![s],\n            None => vec![],\n        };\n\n        self.query_map(&sql, &params, |row| {\n            Ok(Job {\n                id: row.get(0)?,\n                job_type: row.get(1)?,\n                params: row.get(2)?,\n                state: row.get::<_, String>(3)?.parse().map_err(parse_error)?,\n                claimed_by: {\n                    let claimed: String = row.get(4)?;\n                    if claimed.is_empty() {\n                        None\n                    } else {\n                        Some(claimed)\n                    }\n                },\n                claim_expires_at: {\n                    let expires: i64 = row.get(5)?;\n                    if expires == 0 {\n                        None\n                    } else {\n                        Some(expires as u64)\n                    }\n                },\n                progress: row.get(6)?,\n            })\n        })\n    }\n\n    async fn leader_lease_acquire(&self, lease: &LeaderLease) -> Result<bool> {\n        let conn = self\n            .conn\n            .lock()\n            .map_err(|e| TaskStoreError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n        let tx = conn.unchecked_transaction()?;\n\n        let now = chrono::Utc::now().timestamp_millis() as u64;\n\n        // Check if there's an existing valid lease for this scope\n        let existing: Option<(String, u64)> = tx\n            .query_row(\n                \"SELECT scope, expires_at FROM leader_lease WHERE scope = ?1 AND expires_at > ?2\",\n                [&lease.scope as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql, &now as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n                |row| Ok((row.get(0)?, row.get(1)?)),\n            )\n            .ok();\n\n        let acquired = if existing.is_some() {\n            false\n        } else {\n            tx.execute(\n                \"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO leader_lease (scope, holder, expires_at)\n                 VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3)\",\n                [\n                    &lease.scope as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n                    &lease.holder,\n                    &lease.expires_at,\n                ],\n            )?;\n            true\n        };\n\n        tx.commit()?;\n        Ok(acquired)\n    }\n\n    async fn leader_lease_release(&self, scope: &str) -> Result<()> {\n        self.execute(\n            \"DELETE FROM leader_lease WHERE scope = ?1\",\n            &[&scope as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n        )?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn leader_lease_get(&self) -> Result<Option<LeaderLease>> {\n        let result: Option<LeaderLease> = self\n            .query_row(\n                \"SELECT scope, holder, expires_at FROM leader_lease LIMIT 1\",\n                &[] as &[&dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n                |row| {\n                    Ok(LeaderLease {\n                        scope: row.get(0)?,\n                        holder: row.get(1)?,\n                        expires_at: row.get(2)?,\n                    })\n                },\n            )\n            .ok();\n        Ok(result)\n    }\n\n    async fn canary_upsert(&self, canary: &Canary) -> Result<()> {\n        self.execute(\n
